invariants:

notes:
  - [prealloc] prealloc owns the shared semantic-BIR to prealloc-BIR route before MIR lowering
  - [legalize] bootstrap BIR legalize kept semantic CFG and phi form intact while promoting i1 values plus function signature/storage bookkeeping, memory-address/load-store bookkeeping, and call ABI metadata
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'main' with 2 home slot(s) and 8 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout now emits provisional stack objects, elides dead and copy-coalesced home slots, and only allocates frame storage for objects that still require dedicated homes
  - [liveness] liveness now computes BIR named-value intervals, exact def/use program points, predecessor-edge phi uses, call points, CFG-aware live-through extension, and loop depth independently of stack-layout object identity
  - [out_of_ssa] out_of_ssa removed phi nodes from live prepared BIR and published authoritative join-transfer plus parallel-copy obligations
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'main' with 213 allocation constraint(s) and 2565 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 21 register(s) and 192 stack slot(s)

  block entry terminator=branch target=for.cond.1
  block for.cond.1 terminator=cond_branch true=block_1 false=block_2
  block for.latch.1 terminator=branch target=for.cond.1
  block block_1 terminator=branch target=for.cond.3
  block for.cond.3 terminator=cond_branch true=block_3 false=block_4
  block for.latch.3 terminator=branch target=for.cond.3
  block block_2 terminator=return
  block block_3 terminator=branch target=for.latch.3
  block block_4 terminator=branch target=for.latch.1

  branch_condition for.cond.3 kind=fused_compare condition=%t11 compare=ult i64 %t10, %t9 can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_3 false=block_4
